     1	import type {Codec} from './codec';
     2	import type {LogLevel} from './log-level';
     3	import {Log} from './logger';
     4	import {truthy} from './truthy';
     5	
     6	export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
     7	        width,
     8	        height,
     9	        codec,
    10	        scale,
    11	        wantsImageSequence,
    12	        indent,
    13	        logLevel,
    14	}: {
    15	        width: number;
    16	        height: number;
    17	        scale: number;
    18	        codec: Codec;
    19	        wantsImageSequence: boolean;
    20	        indent: boolean;
    21	        logLevel: LogLevel;
    22	}) => {
    23	        let actualWidth = width * scale;
    24	        let actualHeight = height * scale;
    25	        if (wantsImageSequence) {
    26	                return {
    27	                        actualWidth,
    28	                        actualHeight,
    29	                };
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (
    33	                codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
    34	                codec !== 'h264' &&
    35	                codec !== 'h265' &&
    36	                codec !== 'h264-ts'
    37	        ) {
    38	                return {
    39	                        actualWidth,
    40	                        actualHeight,
    41	                };
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        if (
    45	                actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
    46	                (actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
    47	        ) {
    48	                Log.verbose(
    49	                        {indent, logLevel},
    50	                        `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
    51	                );
    52	                actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        if (
    56	                actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
    57	                (actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
    58	        ) {
    59	                Log.verbose(
    60	                        {indent, logLevel},
    61	                        `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
    62	                );
    63	                actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    67	
    68	        if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
    69	                const message = [
    70	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    71	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
    72	                        scale === 1
    73	                                ? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    74	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
    75	                ]
    76	                        .filter(truthy)
    77	                        .join(' ');
    78	                throw new Error(message);
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
    82	                const message = [
    83	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    84	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
    85	                        scale === 1
    86	                                ? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    87	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
    88	                ].join(' ');
    89	                throw new Error(message);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        return {
    93	                actualWidth,
    94	                actualHeight,
    95	        };
    96	};

    22	}) => {
    23	        let actualWidth = width * scale;
    24	        let actualHeight = height * scale;
    25	        if (wantsImageSequence) {
    26	                return {
    27	                        actualWidth,
    28	                        actualHeight,
    29	                };
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (
    33	                codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
    34	                codec !== 'h264' &&
    35	                codec !== 'h265' &&
    36	                codec !== 'h264-ts'
    37	        ) {
    38	                return {
    39	                        actualWidth,
    40	                        actualHeight,
    41	                };
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        if (
    45	                actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
    46	                (actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
    47	        ) {
    48	                Log.verbose(
    49	                        {indent, logLevel},
    50	                        `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
    51	                );
    52	                actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        if (
    56	                actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
    57	                (actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
    58	        ) {
    59	                Log.verbose(
    60	                        {indent, logLevel},
    61	                        `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
    62	                );
    63	                actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    67	
    68	        if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
    69	                const message = [
    70	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    71	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
    72	                        scale === 1
    73	                                ? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    74	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
    75	                ]
    76	                        .filter(truthy)
    77	                        .join(' ');
    78	                throw new Error(message);
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
    82	                const message = [
    83	                        `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    84	                        `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
    85	                        scale === 1
    86	                                ? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    87	                                : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
    88	                ].join(' ');
    89	                throw new Error(message);
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        return {
    93	                actualWidth,
    94	                actualHeight,
    95	        };
    96	};
    97

     1	import type {Codec} from './codec';
     2	import type {LogLevel} from './log-level';
     3	import {Log} from './logger';
     4	import {truthy} from './truthy';
     5	
     6	export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
     7	        width,
     8	        height,
     9	        codec,
    10	        scale,
    11	        wantsImageSequence,
    12	        indent,
    13	        logLevel,
    14	}: {
    15	        width: number;
    16	        height: number;
    17	        scale: number;
    18	        codec: Codec;
    19	        wantsImageSequence: boolean;
    20	        indent: boolean;
    21	        logLevel: LogLevel;
    22	}) => {
    23	        let actualWidth = width * scale;
    24	        let actualHeight = height * scale;
    25	        if (wantsImageSequence) {
    26	                return {
    27	                        actualWidth,
    28	                        actualHeight,
    29	                };
    30	        }
    31	
    32	        if (
    33	                codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
    34	                codec !== 'h264' &&
    35	                codec !== 'h265' &&
    36	                codec !== 'h264-ts'
    37	        ) {
    38	                return {
    39	                        actualWidth,
    40	                        actualHeight,
    41	                };
    42	        }
    43	
    44	        if (
    45	                actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
    46	                (actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
    47	        ) {
    48	                Log.verbose(
    49	                        {indent, logLevel},
    50	                        `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
    51	                );
    52	                actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        if (
    56	                actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
    57	                (actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
    58	        ) {
    59	                Log.verbose(
    60	                        {indent, logLevel},
    61	                        `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
    62	                );
    63	                actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
    67	                if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
    68	                        Log.verbose(
    69	                                {indent, logLevel},
    70	                                `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
    71	                        );
    72	                        actualWidth -= 1;
    73	                } else {
    74	                        const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    75	                        const message = [
    76	                                `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    77	                                `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
    78	                                scale === 1
    79	                                        ? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    80	                                        : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
    81	                        ]
    82	                                .filter(truthy)
    83	                                .join(' ');
    84	                        throw new Error(message);
    85	                }
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
    89	                if (actualHeight % 1 === 0) {
    90	                        Log.verbose(
    91	                                {indent, logLevel},
    92	                                `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${actualHeight - 1}`,
    93	                        );
    94	                        actualHeight -= 1;
    95	                } else {
    96	                        const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    97	                        const message = [
    98	                                `Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    99	                                `The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
   100	                                scale === 1
   101	                                        ? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
   102	                                        : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
   103	                        ].join(' ');
   104	                        throw new Error(message);
   105	                }
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        return {
   109	                actualWidth,
   110	                actualHeight,
   111	        };
   112	};

        width,
        height,
        codec,
        scale,
        wantsImageSequence,
        indent,
        logLevel,
}: {
        width: number;
        height: number;
        scale: number;
        codec: Codec;
        wantsImageSequence: boolean;
        indent: boolean;
        logLevel: LogLevel;
}) => {
        let actualWidth = width * scale;
        let actualHeight = height * scale;
        if (wantsImageSequence) {
                return {
                        actualWidth,
                        actualHeight,
                };
        }

        if (
                codec !== '"'"'h264-mkv'"'"' &&
                codec !== '"'"'h264'"'"' &&
                codec !== '"'"'h265'"'"' &&
                codec !== '"'"'h264-ts'"'"'
        ) {
                return {
                        actualWidth,
                        actualHeight,
                };
        }

        if (
                actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
                (actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
        ) {
                Log.verbose(
                        {indent, logLevel},
                        `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
                );
                actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
        }

                actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
                (actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)

                        {indent, logLevel},
                        `Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
                );
                actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
        }

        if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
                if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
                        Log.verbose(
                                {indent, logLevel},
                                `Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
                        );
                        actualWidth -= 1;
                } else {
                        const displayName = codec === '"'"'h265'"'"' ? '"'"'H265'"'"' : '"'"'H264'"'"';

                                        ? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
                                        : `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
                        ]
                                .filter(truthy)
                                .join('"'"' '"'"');
                        throw new Error(message);
                }
        }

' --new_str 'export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
	width,
	height,
	codec,
	scale,
	wantsImageSequence,
	indent,
	logLevel,
}: {
	width: number;
	height: number;
	scale: number;
	codec: Codec;
	wantsImageSequence: boolean;
	indent: boolean;
	logLevel: LogLevel;
}) => {
	let actualWidth = width * scale;
	let actualHeight = height * scale;
	if (wantsImageSequence) {
		return {
			actualWidth,
			actualHeight,
		};
	}

	if (
		codec !== '"'"'h264-mkv'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h264'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h265'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h264-ts'"'"'
	) {
		return {
			actualWidth,
			actualHeight,
		};
	}

	if (
		actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
		(actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
	) {
		Log.verbose(
			{indent, logLevel},
			`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
		);
		actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
	}

	if (
		actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
		(actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
	) {
		Log.verbose(
			{indent, logLevel},
			`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
		);
		actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
	}

	if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
		if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
			Log.verbose(
				{indent, logLevel},
				`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
			);
			actualWidth -= 1;
		} else {
			const displayName = codec === '"'"'h265'"'"' ? '"'"'H265'"'"' : '"'"'H264'"'"';
			const message = [
				`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
				`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
				scale === 1
					? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
					: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
			]
				.filter(truthy)
				.join('"'"' '"'"');
			throw new Error(message);
		}
	}

	if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
		if (actualHeight % 1 === 0) {
			Log.verbose(
				{indent, logLevel},
				`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${actualHeight - 1}`,
			);
			actualHeight -= 1;
		} else {
			const displayName = codec === '"'"'h265'"'"' ? '"'"'H265'"'"' : '"'"'H264'"'"';
			const message = [
				`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
				`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
				scale === 1
					? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
					: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
			].join('"'"' '"'"');
			throw new Error(message);
		}
	}

	return {
		actualWidth,
		actualHeight,
	};
};

     6	export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
     7	width,
     8	height,
     9	codec,
    10	scale,
    11	wantsImageSequence,
    12	indent,
    13	logLevel,
    14	}: {
    15	width: number;
    16	height: number;
    17	scale: number;
    18	codec: Codec;
    19	wantsImageSequence: boolean;
    20	indent: boolean;
    21	logLevel: LogLevel;
    22	}) => {
    23	let actualWidth = width * scale;
    24	let actualHeight = height * scale;
    25	if (wantsImageSequence) {
    26	return {
    27	actualWidth,
    28	actualHeight,
    29	};
    30	}
    31	
    32	if (
    33	codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
    34	codec !== 'h264' &&
    35	codec !== 'h265' &&
    36	codec !== 'h264-ts'
    37	) {
    38	return {
    39	actualWidth,
    40	actualHeight,
    41	};
    42	}
    43	
    44	if (
    45	actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
    46	(actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
    47	) {
    48	Log.verbose(
    49	{indent, logLevel},
    50	`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
    51	);
    52	actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
    53	}
    54	
    55	if (
    56	actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
    57	(actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
    58	) {
    59	Log.verbose(
    60	{indent, logLevel},
    61	`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
    62	);
    63	actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
    64	}
    65	
    66	if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
    67	if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
    68	Log.verbose(
    69	{indent, logLevel},
    70	`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
    71	);
    72	actualWidth -= 1;
    73	} else {
    74	const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    75	const message = [
    76	`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    77	`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
    78	scale === 1
    79	? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
    80	: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
    81	]
    82	.filter(truthy)
    83	.join(' ');
    84	throw new Error(message);
    85	}
    86	}
    87	
    88	if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
    89	if (actualHeight % 1 === 0) {
    90	Log.verbose(
    91	{indent, logLevel},
    92	`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${actualHeight - 1}`,
    93	);
    94	actualHeight -= 1;
    95	} else {
    96	const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
    97	const message = [
    98	`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
    99	`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
   100	scale === 1
   101	? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
   102	: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
   103	].join(' ');
   104	throw new Error(message);
   105	}
   106	}
   107	
   108	return {
   109	actualWidth,
   110	actualHeight,
   111	};
   112	};
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.

	width,
	height,
	codec,
	scale,
	wantsImageSequence,
	indent,
	logLevel,
}: {
	width: number;
	height: number;
	scale: number;
	codec: Codec;
	wantsImageSequence: boolean;
	indent: boolean;
	logLevel: LogLevel;
}) => {
	let actualWidth = width * scale;
	let actualHeight = height * scale;
	if (wantsImageSequence) {
		return {
			actualWidth,
			actualHeight,
		};
	}

	if (
		codec !== '"'"'h264-mkv'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h264'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h265'"'"' &&
		codec !== '"'"'h264-ts'"'"'
	) {
		return {
			actualWidth,
			actualHeight,
		};
	}

	if (
		actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
		(actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
	) {
		Log.verbose(
			{indent, logLevel},
			`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
		);
		actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
	}

	if (
		actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
		(actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
	) {
		Log.verbose(
			{indent, logLevel},
			`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
		);
		actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
	}

	if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
		if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
			Log.verbose(
				{indent, logLevel},
				`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
			);

			]

No replacement was performed, old_str `export const validateEvenDimensionsWithCodec = ({
width,
height,
codec,
scale,
wantsImageSequence,
indent,
logLevel,
}: {
width: number;
height: number;
scale: number;
codec: Codec;
wantsImageSequence: boolean;
indent: boolean;
logLevel: LogLevel;
}) => {
let actualWidth = width * scale;
let actualHeight = height * scale;
if (wantsImageSequence) {
return {
actualWidth,
actualHeight,
};
}

if (
codec !== 'h264-mkv' &&
codec !== 'h264' &&
codec !== 'h265' &&
codec !== 'h264-ts'
) {
return {
actualWidth,
actualHeight,
};
}

if (
actualWidth % 1 !== 0 &&
(actualWidth % 1 < 0.005 || actualWidth % 1 > 0.005)
) {
Log.verbose(
{indent, logLevel},
`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${Math.round(actualWidth)}`,
);
actualWidth = Math.round(actualWidth);
}

if (
actualHeight % 1 !== 0 &&
(actualHeight % 1 < 0.005 || actualHeight % 1 > 0.005)
) {
Log.verbose(
{indent, logLevel},
`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${Math.round(actualHeight)}`,
);
actualHeight = Math.round(actualHeight);
}

if (actualWidth % 2 !== 0) {
if (actualWidth % 1 === 0) {
Log.verbose(
{indent, logLevel},
`Rounding width to an even number from ${actualWidth} to ${actualWidth - 1}`,
);
actualWidth -= 1;
} else {
const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
const message = [
`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a width of ${actualWidth}px, which is an uneven number.`,
`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two.`,
scale === 1
? `Change the width to ${Math.floor(width - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original width is ${width} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual width.`,
]
.filter(truthy)
.join(' ');
throw new Error(message);
}
}

if (actualHeight % 2 !== 0) {
if (actualHeight % 1 === 0) {
Log.verbose(
{indent, logLevel},
`Rounding height to an even number from ${actualHeight} to ${actualHeight - 1}`,
);
actualHeight -= 1;
} else {
const displayName = codec === 'h265' ? 'H265' : 'H264';
const message = [
`Codec error: You are trying to render a video with a ${displayName} codec that has a height of ${actualHeight}px, which is an uneven number.`,
`The ${displayName} codec does only support dimensions that are evenly divisible by two. `,
scale === 1
? `Change the height to ${Math.floor(actualHeight - 1)}px to fix this issue.`
: `You have used the "scale" option which might be the reason for the problem: The original height is ${height} and the scale is ${scale}x, which was multiplied to get the actual height.`,
].join(' ');
throw new Error(message);
}
}

return {
actualWidth,
actualHeight,
};
};
